                            'position': position + '/' + total
                        }]

                    document.location.href = location;

    <script type="text/javascript">
    var activeAbs = {"62":{"c":"5","d":"95"},"77":{"d":"75","e":"10","f":"10","c":"5"}};
    
    function runAb(name) {
        if ( !activeAbs || !activeAbs[name] ) {
            return null;
        }
        try {
            var cookie_val = $.cookie("aboption");
            if (cookie_val) {
                cookie_val = decodeURIComponent(cookie_val);
            }
            var abOpt = jQuery.parseJSON(cookie_val);
        } catch (e) {}
        if ( abOpt &amp;&amp; abOpt[name] &amp;&amp; activeAbs[name][abOpt[name]] ) {
            return abOpt[name];
        }
        var currentOpt = generateAb(activeAbs[name]);
        if ( currentOpt ) {
            recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt);
        }
        return currentOpt;
    }

    function recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt) {
        if ( !abOpt ) {
            abOpt = {};
        } else {
            $.each(abOpt, function(opt, val) {
                if ( !activeAbs[opt] ) {
                    delete abOpt[opt];
                }
            });
        }
        abOpt[name] = currentOpt;
        $.cookie("aboption", JSON.stringify(abOpt), { path: '/', domain: '.emag.ro', expires: 30 });
        $.ajax({url: "/ablogger.php?name=" + name + "&amp;value=" + currentOpt + "&amp;source=www"});

    }

    function generateAb(distribution) {
        var limit = 0;
        var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 1);
        var curOpt = lastOpt = null;
        $.each(distribution, function(opt, val) {
            lastOpt = opt;
            limit+= parseFloat(val);
            if ( rnd &lt;= limit ) {
                curOpt = opt;
                return false;
            }
        });
        if ( curOpt ) {
            return curOpt;
        } else {
            return lastOpt;
        }
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){
        runAb(53);
        runAb(62);
        runAb(66);
        runAb(57);
        runAb(69);
        runAb(74);
        runAb(77);
    });
</script>

        if ( $.cookie("profile_token") === null ) {
            var currTime = new Date();
            str = currTime.getTime() + '' + Math.random();
            str = str.split('').sort(function(){return 0.5-Math.random()}).join('');

        }
    });

<script>
    $(window).load(function() {
        if (typeof ABcreateCookie != 'function'){
            function ABcreateCookie(name, value, days) {
                var expires = "";
                if (days) {
                    var date = new Date();
                    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                    expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
                }
                document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; domain=; path=/";
            }
        }
        if (typeof readCookie != 'function') {
            function readCookie(name) {
                var nameEQ = name + "=";
                var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i &lt; ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
                }
                return null;
            }
        }

        var abTestingVariants = {};

        var cookieABTestingId = '';
        var cookieVariant = '';

        if ((cookieABTestingId.length) &amp;&amp; (cookieVariant.length)) {
            if (readCookie('E_ABTesting')) {
                try {
                    abTestingVariants = JSON.parse(readCookie('E_ABTesting'));
                } catch (e) {}
            }

            // write cookie and register variant allocation IF cookie is missing OR IF is different from backend cookie
            if (typeof abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] == 'undefined' || abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] !== cookieVariant) {
                abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] = cookieVariant;

                ABcreateCookie('E_ABTesting', JSON.stringify(abTestingVariants), 30);
                try {
                    $.ajax('/ablogger.php?name=&amp;value=&amp;source=');
                } catch (e) {}
            }
        }
    })
</script>

<!-- END Widget product carousel -->
<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var liveWidgetInterval = 30, // interval in seconds for when to get new products
            liveWidgetIntervalID;

        function instantiateCarousel() {
            var carouselConfig = {
                visible: 5,
                step: 5,
                speed: 500,
                autoStart: false,
                timeOut: 3000
            };
            $('#product-carousel-banda-live').emgCarousel(carouselConfig);
        }

        function getCarouselProducts() {
            var products = {};
            var prodList = new Array();
            var i = 0;
            $('.emg-carousel-live-prod').each(function(){
                prodList[i++] = $(this).attr('id');
            });
            products.produse = prodList;

            return products;
        }

        function updateCarousel() {
            var products = getCarouselProducts();
            $.ajax({
                url: '/ajax_live_products',
                type: 'GET',
                data: products,
                cache: true,
                success: handleCarouselUpdateSuccess
            });
        }

        function handleCarouselUpdateSuccess(data) {
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper').removeClass('emg-spinner-wrapper').addClass('emg-spinner-pausedClass');
            var count = (data.match(/&lt;figure/g) || []).length;
            if (count &gt; 0) {
                var width = $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay figure').width();
                $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay').html(data + $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay').html());
                var nrElms = $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay figure').length;
                if(nrElms &gt; 40){
                    $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay').children().filter(":gt(40)").remove();
                }
                $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay figure').css('width',width);
                $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay').css('margin-left', -(width+10)*count + 'px');
                $('#product-carousel-banda-live .emg-carousel-overlay').animate({marginLeft: '-5px'},1000);

                instantiateCarousel();
            }
            setTimeout(handleSpinner, 100);
        }

        function onWindowFocusEventHandler () {
            updateCarousel();
            startLiveWidgetTimer();
            window.removeEventListener('focus', onWindowFocusEventHandler);
        }

        function liveWidgetIntervalHandler() {
            if (document.hasFocus()) {
                updateCarousel();
                return;
            }

            stopLiveWidgetTimer();
            window.addEventListener('focus', onWindowFocusEventHandler);
        }

        function startLiveWidgetTimer() {
            liveWidgetIntervalID = setInterval(liveWidgetIntervalHandler, liveWidgetInterval * 1000);
        }

        function stopLiveWidgetTimer() {
            clearInterval(liveWidgetIntervalID);
        }

        function handleSpinner() {
            $('.emg-spinner-pausedClass').removeClass('emg-spinner-pausedClass-test').addClass('emg-spinner-wrapper');
        }

        function prepareCarouselAnimation(liveWidgetInterval) {
            $('.emg-live-timer span').html(liveWidgetInterval);

            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-filler').css('animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner').css('animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-mask').css('animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');

            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-filler').css('animation-iteration-count', '1');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner').css('animation-iteration-count', '1');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-mask').css('animation-iteration-count', '1');

            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-filler').css('-webkit-animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner').css('-webkit-animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-mask').css('-webkit-animation-duration', liveWidgetInterval + 's');

            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-filler').css('-webkit-animation-iteration-count', '1');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner').css('-webkit-animation-iteration-count', '1');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper .emg-spinner-mask').css('-webkit-animation-iteration-count', '1');
            $('.emg-spinner-wrapper').removeClass('emg-spinner-wrapper').addClass('emg-spinner-pausedClass');

            setTimeout(handleSpinner, 100);
        }

        instantiateCarousel();
        prepareCarouselAnimation(liveWidgetInterval);

        startLiveWidgetTimer();
    });
</script>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                    $(document).ready(function(){
                        $('#carousel-department-widget-1').emgCarousel(
                            {
                                visible: 1,
                                speed: 500,
                                autoStart: false,
                                timeOut: 3000,
                                onChange: function(index) {
                                    var childs      = $(this).find('figure');
                                    var product     = childs.eq(index).find('.gtm-product-details');
                                    var total       = childs.length;
                                    var position    = total - childs.eq(index).nextAll().length;

                                    Emag.DatalayerManager.pushData({
                                        'ecommerce': {
                                            'impressions': [{
                                                'id': product.val(),
                                                'category': product.data('category'),
                                                'position': position+'/'+total,
                                                'list': 'Widget_' + $(this).parents('.emg-dep').find('h3:first-child').text().replace(/[,\s]/g, '_')
                                            }]
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        );
                    });
                </script>

                    $(document).ready(function(){
                        $('#carousel-department-widget-190').emgCarousel(
                            {
                                visible: 1,
                                speed: 500,
                                autoStart: false,
                                timeOut: 3000,
                                onChange: function(index) {
                                    var childs      = $(this).find('figure');
                                    var product     = childs.eq(index).find('.gtm-product-details');
                                    var total       = childs.length;
                                    var position    = total - childs.eq(index).nextAll().length;

                                    Emag.DatalayerManager.pushData({
                                        'ecommerce': {
                                            'impressions': [{
                                                'id': product.val(),
                                                'category': product.data('category'),
                                                'position': position+'/'+total,
                                                'list': 'Widget_' + $(this).parents('.emg-dep').find('h3:first-child').text().replace(/[,\s]/g, '_')
                                            }]
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        );
                    });

                <script type="text/javascript">
                    $(document).ready(function(){
                        $('#carousel-department-widget-23').emgCarousel(
                            {
                                visible: 1,
                                speed: 500,
                                autoStart: false,
                                timeOut: 3000,
                                onChange: function(index) {
                                    var childs      = $(this).find('figure');
                                    var product     = childs.eq(index).find('.gtm-product-details');
                                    var total       = childs.length;
                                    var position    = total - childs.eq(index).nextAll().length;

                                    Emag.DatalayerManager.pushData({
                                        'ecommerce': {
                                            'impressions': [{
                                                'id': product.val(),
                                                'category': product.data('category'),
                                                'position': position+'/'+total,
                                                'list': 'Widget_' + $(this).parents('.emg-dep').find('h3:first-child').text().replace(/[,\s]/g, '_')
                                            }]
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        );
                    });
                </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    function getViewport() {

        var viewPortWidth;
        var viewPortHeight;

        // the more standards compliant browsers (mozilla/netscape/opera/IE7) use window.innerWidth and window.innerHeight
        if (typeof window.innerWidth != 'undefined') {
            viewPortWidth = window.innerWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = window.innerHeight
        }

        // IE6 in standards compliant mode (i.e. with a valid doctype as the first line in the document)
        else if (typeof document.documentElement != 'undefined'
                &amp;&amp; typeof document.documentElement.clientWidth !=
                'undefined' &amp;&amp; document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0) {
            viewPortWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight
        }

        // older versions of IE
        else {
            viewPortWidth = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientHeight
        }
        return viewPortWidth + 'x' + viewPortHeight;
    }

    function createCookie(name,value,days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
            var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        }
        else var expires = "";
        document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
    }

    var screenResolution = window.screen.availWidth + 'x' + window.screen.availHeight;
    var viewPort = getViewport();

    createCookie('sr',screenResolution,365);
    createCookie('vp',viewPort,365);

    if($.cookie("_rsv") == null){
        var rsv = 1;
    } else {
        var rsv = eval($.cookie("_rsv")) + 1;
    }
    $.cookie("_rsv", rsv, { expires: 1, path:"/"});

    if($.cookie("_rsv") &gt;= 2){
        $.cookie("_rscd", 1, { expires: 1, path:"/"});
    }

    if($.cookie("_rsv") != null){
        var rsdc = eval($.cookie("_rscd")) + 1;
        $.cookie("_rsdc", rsdc, { expires: 3, path:"/"});
    }

    $(window).load(function(){
        if (typeof(GUI) !== "object"){
            $.getScript("https://s0emagst.akamaized.net/layout/ro/www/js/assetic/gui-55aec2d.js");
        }
        else{ 
            $(document).trigger('gui-init'); 
        }
        try {
            $.postLogin();
        }catch(e){
            console.info('PostLogin not defined');
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function get_browser_version(){
        var N=navigator.appName, ua=navigator.userAgent, tem;
        var M=ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie)\/?\s*(\.?\d+(\.\d+)*)/i);
        if(M &amp;&amp; (tem= ua.match(/version\/([\.\d]+)/i))!= null) M[2]= tem[1];
        M=M? [M[1], M[2]]: [N, navigator.appVersion, '-?'];
        return parseInt(M[1]);
    }
